style="-sec-extract:summary;margin-bottom:9pt;padding-left:72pt;text-indent:-72pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 3.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Unregistered Sales of Equity Securities.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On September 15, 2025, Intel Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) entered into a Securities Purchase Agreement (the &#8220;Purchase Agreement&#8221;) with NVIDIA Corporation (&#8220;NVIDIA&#8221;) pursuant to which NVIDIA agreed to purchase 214,776,632 shares of the Company&#8217;s common stock, par value $0.001 per share (the &#8220;Shares&#8221;), at $23.28 per share, representing an aggregate purchase price in cash of $5.0 billion. The Shares are to be issued in a private placement in reliance on the exemption provided by Section 4(a)(2) of the Securities Act of 1933 as a transaction not involving a public offering.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Purchase Agreement contains customary representations, warranties and covenants, and the closing of the transaction is subject to customary closing conditions, including the expiration of any applicable waiting periods, and receipt of any required approvals, under the Hart-Scott-Rodino Antitrust Improvements Act of 1976. The Purchase Agreement does not provide for any governance or information rights beyond those applicable to Intel shareholders generally.</span></div><div id="ic7644a3d93a64ccc85c1832cb5691e1b_10"></div><div style="-sec-extract:summary;margin-bottom:9pt;padding-left:72pt;text-indent:-72pt"><span announcing the private placement contemplated by the Purchase Agreement and a collaboration between Intel and NVIDIA to develop AI infrastructure and personal computing products is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The information in Item 7.01 of this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1, is furnished and shall not be treated as filed for purposes of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended.</span></div><div id="ic7644a3d93a64ccc85c1832cb5691e1b_13"></div><div NVIDIA to invest $5 billion in Intel common stock</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">SANTA CLARA, Calif., Sept. 18, 2025 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- NVIDIA (NASDAQ&#58; NVDA) and Intel Corporation (NASDAQ&#58; INTC) today announced a collaboration to jointly develop multiple generations of custom data center and PC products that accelerate applications and workloads across hyperscale, enterprise and consumer markets.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The companies will focus on seamlessly connecting NVIDIA and Intel architectures using NVIDIA NVLink &#8212; integrating the strengths of NVIDIA&#8217;s AI and accelerated computing with Intel&#8217;s leading CPU technologies and x86 ecosystem to deliver cutting-edge solutions for customers.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For data centers, Intel will build NVIDIA-custom x86 CPUs that NVIDIA will integrate into its AI infrastructure platforms and offer to the market.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For personal computing, Intel will build and offer to the market x86 system-on-chips (SOCs) that integrate NVIDIA RTX GPU chiplets. These new x86 RTX SOCs will power a wide range of PCs that demand integration of world-class CPUs and GPUs.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NVIDIA will invest $5 billion in Intel&#8217;s common stock at a purchase price of $23.28 per share. The investment is subject to customary closing conditions, including required regulatory approvals.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;AI is powering a new industrial revolution and reinventing every layer of the computing stack &#8212; from silicon to systems to software. At the heart of this reinvention is NVIDIA&#8217;s CUDA architecture,&#8221; said NVIDIA founder and CEO Jensen Huang. &#8220;This historic collaboration tightly couples NVIDIA&#8217;s AI and accelerated computing stack with Intel&#8217;s CPUs and the vast x86 ecosystem &#8212; a fusion of two world-class platforms. Together, we will expand our ecosystems and lay the foundation for the next era of computing.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;Intel&#8217;s x86 architecture has been foundational to modern computing for decades &#8212; and we are innovating across our portfolio to enable the workloads of the future,&#8221; said Lip-Bu Tan, CEO of Intel. &#8220;Intel&#8217;s leading data center and client computing platforms, combined with our process technology, manufacturing and advanced packaging capabilities, will complement NVIDIA&#8217;s AI and accelerated computing leadership to enable new breakthroughs for the industry. We appreciate the confidence Jensen and the NVIDIA team have placed in us with their investment and look forward to the work ahead as we innovate for customers and grow our business.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Press Conference&#58; </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The CEOs of NVIDIA and Intel will conduct a webcast press conference at 10 a.m. Pacific time (1 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss the announcement.
